Now let me create all three test files. Let me carefully design them based on the `syscall_new_thread` specification:

Key spec to test:
- **`syscall_new_thread`**: requires `wf()`, `thread_dom().contains(thread_ptr)`; ensures `wf()`, `syscall_new_thread_requirement(*old(self), thread_ptr) == false <==> ret.is_error()`
- **`syscall_new_thread_requirement`**: checks thread list not full, quota > 0, scheduler not full, free pages > 0
- **`new_thread`**: postconditions about domain changes, quota subtraction, process preservation
- **`alloc_page_4k`**: requires `wf()`, `free_pages_4k.len() > 0`
- **`page_ptr2page_index`**: requires `ptr % 0x1000 == 0`
- **`page_index2page_ptr`**: requires `0 <= i < NUM_PAGES`
- **`NoSwitchNew`**: ensures error_code, pcid, cr3, switch_decision

Now I have a thorough understanding. Let me create the three test files for `share_mapping`. The key function to test is `share_mapping` which shares a page mapping from one process to another.

Key preconditions (`requires`) of `share_mapping`:
1. `old(self).wf()` - kernel well-formed
2. `old(self).proc_dom().contains(src_proc_ptr)` - src proc exists
3. `old(self).proc_dom().contains(target_proc_ptr)` - target proc exists
4. `va_4k_valid(target_va)` - target VA is valid 4k
5. `old(self).page_alloc.page_is_mapped(entry.addr)` - page is mapped
6. `page_ptr_valid(entry.addr)` - page ptr is valid
7. `old(self).get_address_space(src_proc_ptr).dom().contains(src_va)` - src VA is mapped in src proc
8. `old(self).get_address_space(src_proc_ptr)[src_va].addr == entry.addr` - entry addr matches src
9. `old(self).get_address_space(target_proc_ptr).dom().contains(target_va) == false` - target VA NOT mapped
10. L2 resolution exists and matches tagret_l1_p
11. `old(self).get_physical_page_reference_counter(entry.addr) <= usize::MAX - 1` - ref counter won't overflow

Key postconditions (`ensures`):
- `self.wf()` preserved
- Domains preserved (proc, thread, endpoint, container)
- Free pages count unchanged
- Procs unchanged
- Other procs' address spaces unchanged
- Target proc's address space = old + insert(target_va, entry)
- Page mapping: only entry.addr changes (insert (target_proc_ptr, target_va))
- Reference counter of entry.addr incremented by 1
- Other pages' ref counters unchanged

- **Logical (12/12 FAIL)**: Unentailed properties (determinism, domain preservation, return value specifics, thread state transitions) are properly rejected

**Key finding**: `syscall_send_empty_block`'s postcondition (`ensures self.wf()`) is very weak — it preserves well-formedness but doesn't propagate the rich guarantees of its helper functions (`schedule_blocked_thread`, `block_running_thread_*`) to callers.

Now I have a thorough understanding of the target function `helper_kernel_kill_proc_root`. Let me analyze the key specs:

**Preconditions (requires):**
1. `old(self).wf()` — kernel well-formed
2. `old(self).proc_dom().contains(proc_ptr)` — proc must exist
3. `old(self).get_proc(proc_ptr).ioid.is_None()` — no IO id
4. `old(self).mem_man.get_pagetable_by_pcid(old(self).get_proc(proc_ptr).pcid).unwrap().is_empty()` — pagetable empty
5. `old(self).get_proc(proc_ptr).owned_threads@ == Seq::<ThreadPtr>::empty()` — no threads
6. `old(self).get_proc(proc_ptr).children@ == Seq::<ProcPtr>::empty()` — no children
7. `old(self).get_proc(proc_ptr).depth == 0` — must be root (depth 0)

**Postconditions (ensures):**
1. `self.wf()` — kernel still well-formed
2. `self.thread_dom() == old(self).thread_dom()` — threads unchanged
3. `threads_unchanged_except(old(self).proc_man, self.proc_man, set![])` — no thread exceptions
4. `self.proc_dom() == old(self).proc_dom().remove(proc_ptr)` — proc removed
5. `processes_fields_unchanged(old(self).proc_man, self.proc_man)` — remaining proc fields same
6. `self.container_dom() == old(self).container_dom()` — containers unchanged
7. `containers_tree_unchanged(old(self).proc_man, self.proc_man)` — container tree same
8. Pagetable mappings preserved for remaining procs
9. Children unchanged for remaining procs
10. Subtree set updated for upper-tree procs
11. Uppertree seq unchanged for remaining procs
